                product.requiredProducts.forEach(function(requiredProduct, index) {

                });
            });
        };

        gogEventBus.subscribe("cart", "updated", function(eventData) {
            setTimeout(function() {
                reloadDependencies();
            }, 200);
        });

        reloadDependencies();
